				<article id="post-3168" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-3168 page type-page status-publish hentry">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3168_6f51f9-10"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="1000" height="500" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500-260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500_2-1.jpg" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-4793" srcset="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500-260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500_2-1.jpg 1000w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500-260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500_2-1-300x150.jpg 300w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500-260219_GRAPHICS-5638_Career-page_1000X500_2-1-768x384.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px"></figure></div>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_12f210-78 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_5abad4-63"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_8e60e5-e5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_d5b748-2f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Life at flaconi</h1>



<p class="has-text-align-center lila-hg has-medium-font-size"><strong><strong>We Deliver Moments of Beauty That Spark Joy</strong></strong></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-3168_244a76-30"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_b51ad4-0d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="kt-adv-heading3168_6dbb68-b3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_6dbb68-b3">This vision drives us. It’s not only about the individual moments and the feelings they evoke – though those are central – but also about the we behind it all.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading3168_d493a0-66 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_d493a0-66">#WeCommerce is what we do. For us, this means bringing customers, colleagues, and partners together in harmony. This core idea shapes our decisions, our actions, and our company culture.</p>



<p>With our Code of Ethics, company values, and Leadership Standards, we have created key building blocks that help us continuously foster this core principle. These cultural pillars provide the framework and strengthen all our initiatives, making flaconi an exceptional place to be.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_841679-0c alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_7a3db2-b4"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading3168_d089ff-64 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-6-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_d089ff-64">The way we work</h1>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-3168_ef9782-af"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"></div></div>



<p class="kt-adv-heading3168_558baa-64 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_558baa-64">To empower our employees to achieve optimal work-life balance, we developed three flexible working models:</p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_4f5871-e0 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_422542-89"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3168_954bfd-cd is-resized"><figure class="alignleft size-full"><img decoding="async" width="100" height="100" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/Traveller-2.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-2989"></figure></div>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3168_939b42-ce wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_939b42-ce">#Traveller</h2>



<p>Our hybrid model combines the freedom of remote work with the benefits of office presence. flaconis who choose this model work primarily remote but come into the office for <strong>eight days per month</strong>. How you distribute these days is entirely up to you, offering the flexibility to ensure that work fits your life, not the other way around.</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_224229-9b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3168_955060-df is-resized"><figure class="alignleft size-full"><img decoding="async" width="100" height="100" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/Settler-1.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-2987"></figure></div>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3168_8be960-00 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_8be960-00">#Settler</h2>



<p>This model is perfect for those who prefer the office as their primary workspace and value direct, in-person interaction. You will work <strong>on-site four days a week</strong>, with the flexibility to work <strong>remotely one day a week</strong>. This way, you get the full office experience while maintaining the freedom to shape your schedule.</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_4e360c-be"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3168_f985ac-c8 is-resized"><figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="100" height="100" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/Astronaut-1.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-2991"></figure></div>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3168_600a37-5c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_600a37-5c">#Astronaut</h2>



<p>Our remote model is perfect for flaconis who live <strong>outside of Berlin </strong>and prefer to work entirely from home. As we foster an “In-Person-First” culture, this model is available for selected individual contributor roles. The only requirement is that your place of residence and work must be located within Germany.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p class="kt-adv-heading3168_8bf458-ed wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_8bf458-ed"></p>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3168_1026a5-c2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_1026a5-c2">Our Benefits</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_ddb72c-ab alignwide wp-block-kadence-rowlayout" id="benefits"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-4-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-two-grid kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_d30d4f-b6"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-flipbox-flipbox-block"><div class="eb-parent-wrapper eb-parent-eb-flipbox-stvuq "><div class="eb-flipbox-container eb-flipbox-stvuq eb-hover-mode" data-id="eb-flipbox-stvuq" data-flip-type="flip-left" data-flip-mode="hover"><div class="eb-flipper flip-left"><div class="eb-flipbox-front"><div class="eb-flipbox-items-container"><div class="eb-flipbox-icon-wrapper"><div class="eb-flipbox-front-image-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/230131-BVG.png" alt=""></div></div><div class="eb-flipbox-front-title-wrapper"><h3 class="eb-flipbox-front-title">Public Transport Ticket</h3></div></div></div><div class="eb-flipbox-back"><div class="eb-flipbox-items-container"><div class="eb-flipbox-back-content-wrapper"><p class="eb-flipbox-back-content">Getting around Berlin or Halle is on us! We subsidize your public transport ticket, so you can enjoy a stress-free commute and explore the city</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_7083e4-83"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-flipbox-flipbox-block"><div class="eb-parent-wrapper eb-parent-eb-flipbox-tkg2m "><div class="eb-flipbox-container eb-flipbox-tkg2m eb-hover-mode" data-id="eb-flipbox-tkg2m" data-flip-type="flip-left" data-flip-mode="hover"><div class="eb-flipper flip-left"><div class="eb-flipbox-front"><div class="eb-flipbox-items-container"><div class="eb-flipbox-icon-wrapper"><div class="eb-flipbox-front-image-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/230131-sport.png" alt="flaconi Fitness"></div></div><div class="eb-flipbox-front-title-wrapper"><h3 class="eb-flipbox-front-title">Urban Sports Club And Other Fitness Offers</h3></div></div></div><div class="eb-flipbox-back"><div class="eb-flipbox-items-container"><div class="eb-flipbox-back-content-wrapper"><p class="eb-flipbox-back-content">Time to break a sweat! With our subsidized Urban Sports Club membership and our own on-site gym, you can find the perfect work-life balance through fitness, yoga, and more.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_c429cb-80"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Win-as-a-Team </strong><br>We recognize and celebrate everyone’s accomplishments.</p>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_374e26-99 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_374e26-99">Code of Ethics</h2>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-3621_2dcf2c-d2"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"></div></div>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_387253-a3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_387253-a3">#compliance</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We comply with the law. With no exception. We understand it is our responsibility to be informed about legal boundaries.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3621_9e035e-a2 splide__slide splide__slide--clone" id="splide02-clone02" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(33.3333% - 20px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap kb-slide-align-null kb-slide-valign-top"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3621_19107b-07 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3621_78c3c6-b4"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3621_4d96bc-59 size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="64" height="64" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/ethic-respekt.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-751"></figure>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_4242fb-d7 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_4242fb-d7">#respect</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We treat everybody with respect and dignity. We demand honesty and tolerance for different opinions and beliefs.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3621_abac71-d5 splide__slide splide__slide--clone" id="splide02-clone03" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(33.3333% - 20px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap kb-slide-align-null kb-slide-valign-top"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3621_416af7-8f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3621_2255a8-8a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3621_7d6bd2-62 is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="64" height="64" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/ethic-gleichheit.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-743"></figure>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_dcc554-08 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_dcc554-08">#equality</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We believe all humans are created equal. We do not discriminate on the basis of gender, race, age, religion, origin, disability or sexual orientation. We believe diversity makes us stronger – personally and professionally.  </p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3621_9084a0-38 splide__slide splide__slide--clone" id="splide02-clone04" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(33.3333% - 20px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap kb-slide-align-null kb-slide-valign-top"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3621_f4ad3f-0c alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3621_c98f03-8b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3621_ed4fe3-73"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="64" height="61" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/ethic-nachhaltigkeit.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-741"></figure>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_289e90-65 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_289e90-65">#sustainability</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We act responsibly and sustainably when using the resources of our planet.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3621_b812c9-dc splide__slide splide__slide--clone" id="splide02-clone05" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(33.3333% - 20px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap kb-slide-align-null kb-slide-valign-top"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3621_28e0bc-db alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3621_3e65f7-d6"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3621_4a5d64-7b is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="64" height="64" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/ethic-zusammenhalt.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-747"></figure>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_4a57ca-a6 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_4a57ca-a6">#cohesion</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We speak up for anybody that raises a breach of this code. We commit to listen to others that speak up. We protect all those that speak up.  </p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3621_fb238e-97 splide__slide splide__slide--clone is-prev" id="splide02-clone06" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(33.3333% - 20px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap kb-slide-align-null kb-slide-valign-top"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3621_066e56-14 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3621_af019f-a0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image3621_41b22b-9d is-resized"><figure class="alignleft"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/ethic-verpflichtung.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-749"></figure></div>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_8b7047-8a wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_8b7047-8a">#commitment</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We pledge to individually comply with and hold each other accountable to this standard.</p>
</div></div>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3621_4229ad-58 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3621_4229ad-58">#freedom</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">We commit ourselves to the basic principles of free democratic order.</p>
</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_b46729-26 aligncenter wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3168_aac44b-0c splide__slide splide__slide--clone is-prev" id="splide03-clone01" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(100% + 0px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_23fef9-1a alignnone has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-equal kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_a06847-f7"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="kt-adv-heading3168_dce406-85 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_dce406-85"><strong>#pushforsuccess</strong></h3>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Speed counts </strong><br>We take decisions fast and encourage a results driven implementation. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Be accountable </strong><br>We take responsibility for our teams and celebrate their success </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Disagree and commit </strong><br>We bravely disagree but equally accept and commit to aligned decisions.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Leadership Standards 3/3</strong></p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_9dcfb7-0f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1011" height="1024" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/pushforsuccess-1011x1024.png" alt="" class="wp-image-2090" style="width:297px" srcset="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/pushforsuccess-1011x1024.png 1011w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/pushforsuccess-296x300.png 296w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/pushforsuccess-768x778.png 768w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/pushforsuccess-1517x1536.png 1517w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/pushforsuccess-2023x2048.png 2023w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1011px) 100vw, 1011px"></figure>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3168_7d4a7c-ee splide__slide is-active is-visible" id="splide03-slide01" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(100% + 0px);"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_f3e36f-7a alignnone has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-equal kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_0f9788-47"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="kt-adv-heading3168_49fc26-bd wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_49fc26-bd"><strong>#leadbyexample</strong></h3>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Walk the talk </strong><br>We take full accountability for what we commit to and are consistent in our actions. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Revise with pride </strong><br>We are self-reflected admit mistakes and correct our course. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Give orientation </strong><br>We align on ambitious goals and empower our teams to succeed.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Leadership Standards 1/3</strong></p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_8ac1ac-c3"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="2244" height="2273" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample.png" alt="" class="wp-image-2094" style="width:297px;height:auto" srcset="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample.png 2244w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample-296x300.png 296w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample-1011x1024.png 1011w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample-768x778.png 768w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample-1516x1536.png 1516w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/leadbyexample-2022x2048.png 2022w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 2244px) 100vw, 2244px"></figure>
</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3168_118ca5-e1 splide__slide is-next" id="splide03-slide02" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(100% + 0px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_57a5dc-7a alignnone has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-equal kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_902974-95"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="kt-adv-heading3168_2b396d-55 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_2b396d-55"><strong>#growteams</strong></h3>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Take time to lead </strong><br>We grow individual talent and build successful teams by coaching and challenging. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Exchange feedback </strong><br>We give positive and constructive feedback in an honest, timely and frequent manner. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Challenge each other </strong><br>We don’t hesitate to challenge others in order to achieve better results.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Leadership Standards 2/3</strong></p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_98d79e-16"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="2222" height="2250" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams.png" alt="" class="wp-image-2088" style="width:297px" srcset="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams.png 2222w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams-296x300.png 296w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams-1011x1024.png 1011w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams-768x778.png 768w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams-1517x1536.png 1517w, https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/growteams-2023x2048.png 2023w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 2222px) 100vw, 2222px"></figure>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-slide kb-advanced-slide-item kb-slide-3168_aac44b-0c splide__slide" id="splide03-slide03" role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" aria-label="%1$s of %2$s" style="margin-right: 30px; width: calc(100% + 0px);" aria-hidden="true"><div class="kb-advanced-slide"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner-wrap"><div class="kb-advanced-slide-inner"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3168_23fef9-1a alignnone has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-equal kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_a06847-f7"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="kt-adv-heading3168_dce406-85 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_dce406-85"><strong>#pushforsuccess</strong></h3>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Speed counts </strong><br>We take decisions fast and encourage a results driven implementation. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Be accountable </strong><br>We take responsibility for our teams and celebrate their success </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Disagree and commit </strong><br>We bravely disagree but equally accept and commit to aligned decisions.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>Leadership Standards 3/3</strong></p>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-3168_e30ab6-90"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"></div></div>



<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Responsibility</h1>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3624_419775-6e alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_bbeffa-94"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="kt-adv-heading3624_3913d1-d8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3624_3913d1-d8">Every company must take responsibility for the impact of its actions—whether social, environmental, or economic. At flaconi, we take all aspects of sustainability seriously, as we are committed to actively and responsibly shaping the future of our industry.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3624_10e8ec-fb alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-equal kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_8ae037-28"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Environmental Responsibility</strong></h2>



<p>Developing innovative packaging, avoiding plastic, and ensuring products arrive safely and resource-efficiently is a challenge we embrace. Today, our flaconi shipping boxes are <strong>100% plastic-free</strong>. As a member of the <strong>Forest Stewardship Council (FSC)</strong>, we are committed to using 100% recycled packaging materials.</p>



<p>Our commitment extends to our infrastructure: Our logistics center runs on <strong>100% renewable energy</strong>, and we fully offset the emissions from our heating systems. At our headquarters, we further reduce our carbon footprint through <strong>Smart Heating and Smart Lighting</strong> solutions.</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_3c2c97-3f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3624_dee900-fc alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-equal kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kt-inner-column-height-full kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_ede997-01"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_0bf22d-82"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading" style="line-height:1.2"><strong><strong>Social Responsibility</strong></strong></h2>



<p>Diversity makes us better: it opens up new perspectives and allows everyone to discover their true self and embrace their individuality. Our culture is shaped by <strong>openness, tolerance, and curiosity.</strong> We actively promote talent and diversity while prioritizing the physical and mental health and overall well-being of our colleagues.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3624_7d0e23-1b alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_b5141a-39"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3624_1d1e80-1d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_b673aa-db"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong>Our Vision for the Future</strong></p>



<p>We believe in the skills and dedication of our teams to develop innovative ideas for a shared future. As a company, we are fully aware of our responsibility to make sustainable decisions at every level and to actively stand up for a diverse society. We are working hard to empower our customers to make sustainable purchasing decisions that respect both nature and people alike.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">This is just the beginning. We are constantly striving to find innovative and sustainable solutions for our colleagues, partners, and customers. We certainly won’t get everything perfect right away—but as “flaconis,” we are determined to do our part. Because great goals can only be achieved together.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3624_dc4730-30"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3168_5778fd-f6"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Events</h1>



<p class="kt-adv-heading3168_794175-98 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3168_794175-98">As a company and as individual flaconi employees, we do a lot every day to not only promote our culture but also to fulfill our responsibilities. Therefore, we would like to share some insights with you:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-3168_75aad9-b8"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"></div></div>
